lette flee downe winde almaines doe flee pye leaſe twoo caſte falcon make mownte ſtowpe doe ryuer muſte playne tree woodde little ſhrubbes buſhes vſe giue hawke brekefaſt beaching timely ye morning wil make hir eager flee ſuche time conuenient hir flee eſpecially falcon whiche woulde haue high fleeing thoſe ſhoulde highly kepte ſhoulde fedde nyne dayes togyther sunne riſing nyghte late freſhe coole euening ſhall make highe fleeing meanes wyll euery daye get gate higher higher ſo yt flowen euermore playne champaygne falcon gentle commonly better inwarde ſhe hath mewed hir ſoarage falcon kill hearne naturally ſhe peregrine falcon yet ſhall well giue traynes falcon may flee ten flightes riuer one day ſeaſon extreme moſte ſhall flee hir falcon whiche ryuer hawkes ſhoulde alwaies borne vpon fiſte hawke ſhall haue forty caſtings ſhe perfectly made hawke whiche hath caſting euery nighte ſurcharged abundance ſuperfluitie humor whiche ſtomacke ſo ouerflow brayne cannot flee ſo high elſe would therefore hawkes ſhould haue caſting euery night naturally woulde haue ſounde cleane good giue tyring plumage nighte eſpecially field hawkes ryuer hawkes weakening backes euery thirde daye ſhall preſent water longeſt touche hawkes fethers litle muche handling make order vyllaine lanerette may ſette vpon ſtone incontinently ſoone made hawke hath flowen bated feede hir long ſhee panteth bloweth vntill ſhe breath agayne ſhould perilous bring hir diſeaſe called astma hawke pantiſe hawke eyther falcon chaunce heart diſcouraged happeneth oftentymes take ſuche paynes hir ſhee may kill ſome praye feede hir vp vpon full gorge euen long ſhe eate ſame night ſette hir abroade ſhe may ieouke open ayre hir pleaſure morrowe take hir feede hir ſmall birdes enſeame hir neyther leſſe would hawke newe drawen mewe falcon hawke ſeaze gorge take quill wilde gooſes feather tye vnder hir long ſingle ſhe ſeaze grype ſhe beginneth feaze take away ſayde quyll ſhee ſeaze long afterwards cannot giue couert falcon goſhawke caſte hir sunne hir backe hawkes may made flee ye ſowrce ſpring ſorte ſoeuer flee goſhawke lette hir haue sunne backe flee manner fowles traines partridge rookes crowes chough ſhoulde bee ſeeled nowe enter hawke make lyttle pytte hole grounde putte trayne therein couer hole little borde whiche ſhall faſten ſmall cryaunce corde ſhall holde hande drawe away lyſt thē ſhall make though vncoupled ſpanels hunte put vp game ſhall carry hawke vnhooded perceiue hawke looketh way haue layed trayne drawe borde cauſe traine ſpring though ſpanels ſprong hawke take let hir feede thereon hir fill vpon grounde thus muſt ſundry time woulde haue good hawke nowſel hir yong ſo ſhe encreaſe hir force little little ende ſhee ouercomme bothe feaſaunte partridge c ſhee hath killed loue praye better ſhee killeth henne kinde lette hir plume vpon gyue hir heart brayne moſte bicauſe ſhe ſhall loue flee henne ſo well cocke muche better nouſel hawkes yong fowles olde moſte commonly yong hawke let flee olde game ſhee turne tayle cowardly giue ouer vnleſſe declared woulde nouſel enter haggarde enter hir ſette hir bloude vpon yong praye inure hir thereto ſhe woulde afterwardes paſſe muche olde game likewiſe ſame conſideration ſhall nouſel enter mewed hawke yong game goſhawke fowles generally good traynes crane buſtarde hearne wilde gooſe riuer fowle cormorantes choughes make goſhawke brooke lette hir flee thoſe traynes afore ſayde haue tolde ſee hawke approche fowle within daunger ſtrike vp drumme ſuch time ye fowle eſpie goſhawke ſhe ſee hawke ſhee ſpring ſhe meanes belle according hugeneſſe condition hawke muſt alſo haue hoode hir therewithall muſt oftentymes hoode vnhoode hir ſuch ſort ſhee afrayde thereof hir keeper hee handleth hir nine nightes hee ſhoulde bountifully whyles hawke vpon lewre go aboute hir fayre ſoftly lewring cry wó hó hó falconer vſe haue thus done ſpace certaine dayes take lewre garniſhed ſayde euery day call hir farre ſhee may well heare perceyue let hir looſe hir furniture without either loynes cryaunce ſhe come ſo farre feed rewarde hir well ſtoppe hir hir feeding oftentymes make hir come better take heede hurt hir ſo ſhall alſo ſometymes call hir horſebacke haue vſed hir thus moneth vntill ſhe come well roundly ſhee familiar man without ſtraungeneſſe coyneſſe may ſtop lewre vpon hir make hir flee vpon ſo ſhall meete bathe hir leaſt ſhe libertie ſhe rangle ſeeke water ſo might leeſe hawke euery ſeuen eight dayes hawke ſhould ſet water nature ſo requireth haue thus manned reclaymed lewred falcon go hir fieldes whiſtle hir fyſt ſtanding ſtill ſee ſhe whether ſhe rake ſhe flee rounde vpon good hawke ſhoulde flee let hir flee turne two whiche done throwe hir lewre let hir foote henne pullet kill feede hir well therevppon vnhoode hir often beare hir ceaſe ſo vntill ſhe haue endewed mewted ſufficiently falcon thus made manned go abrode hir euery morning weather fayre calme chuſe place hir flee ſome narrow brooke plaſhe water caſt hir go winde ſo farre fowle may deſcrie ſhe caſt beginneth recouer hir gate make towardes brooke fowle lie alwayes wyling making hawke leane vpon perceiue ſhe reaſonable may better knowe hande remember neuer flee yong hawke without ſome quicke thing caryed field ſhe faile firſt kill wilde fowle may yet make hir kil traine bring ſhall doe certaine time vntill hawke many menned ſpeake diſeaſe pantas dyuerſely yet knowe ſhewe three maner pantaſes wherewith hawkes diſeaſed firſt gorge ſeconde commeth colde thirde reynes kidney firſt kinde pantas commeth bating vpon perche vpon fyſt beareth meanes whereof ſome little veynes liuer breake bloud poureth vppon liuer dryeth cloddeth ſmall flake thoſe ryſing vp afterwarde hawke bateth agayne doe ſtoppe paſſages windepype thereof commeth pantas ſometyme hawke bateth thoſe flake doe ſo aſcende hir throte lie ouerthwart ſhee preſently falleth downe deade inſomuche ſome holde opinion pantas maketh hawkes dye ſodenly proofe whereof open hawke ſhee deade yee ſhall finde maladie hir throte maiſter amé caſsian gyueth medicine thys pantas gorge bycauſe cannot miniſtred hir neither hir throte otherwiſe diſeaſe holdeth hir verie windepipe whereby breath paſſeth neuertheleſſe counſell cloze vp hawke ſome conuenient chamber lattis windowes ſo ſhee may get ſet hir two three perch ſhee may flee one another haue sunne ſhine vpon hir poſſible ſhe muſt haue alwayes water hir yee feede hir hir meate muſt cut ſmall pellet haue neyther feather bone leaſt ſhe ſtreyne hirſelfe tyring ſhe muſt haue halfe gorge day counſell aduice miſchiefe pantas commeth colde pantas commeth colde hawkes take wet fleeing fielde riuer weathered afterwarde ſet place may ſtande warme againe diſeaſe commeth ſtanding ſmoke duſt may annoy ye ſhall knowe pantas hawkes panting ſhee cannot drawe hir breath ſhee ſhould mallopin ſayth remedie diſeaſe ye muſte take filing yron meale lentil eche like quantitie muſt temper togither honie till bee lyke paaſte ye may make little balles bigge peaze whereof ſhall giue hawke two three euery morning noone feede hir good meate beefe dyet ſhall allowe hir three foure dayes ſhe amende ſeaſon hawke throughly recured pantas reynes kidney happeneth ſometymes hawke hath bene recouered ſome great greefe good keeping intendance afterwarde ſhe waxeth euill againe falleth panting wherof breedeth diſeaſe reynes kidney maner canker bigge beane ſwelleth bigger bigger ſuch wiſe ſhee falleth caſting ſome part hir meate pantas differeth muche leaue hir ſeuen eight dayes vexe hir ſtrongly ſomtymes take hir moneth moneth ſo ſhee ſhall beare oute whole yeare diſcerned ſhee panteth ſhee ſtirreth hir reynes hir pinion whereas ſhee ſtyrreth hir pinion hir reynes againe knowe truely commeth goeth euerie ſeuen eight dayes hawke chaunce die rippe hir ſhall finde knubbe bigneſſe ſmall beane full vpon reynes ſmall hir backe whereof diſeaſe proceedeth maiſter caſsian gyueth remedie yee muſt take rootes caper fenell smallage parſley boyle togither newe potte conſumption thirde parte take olde tyle older better make powder thereof ſerue hawke feede hir fleſhe ſtieped water ſayde rootes quarter houre thereaboutes aforehande morning ye giue hir waſht meate giue hir none powder night waſhe hir meate ſayde water beſprinckle powder ſo competently ſhe maye receyue giue hir time aboue halfe gorge let done nine tenne dayes yee ſee hawke amende continue ſtill diſeaſe verie much confirmed hawke borne long hard bee cured yee take diſeaſe newe greene plye hir diligently medicine helpe hir hawke morfounded ſome miſchaunce morfound frenche worde doth ſignifie engliſh taking coldesometimes falleth hawkes morfounded ſome miſchaunce ſometimes alſo giuing great gorge ſpecially wette cannot indewe put ouer theyr gorge ſo ſurfeyte bycauſe meate conuerteth ſlyme groſſe humour ouerthrowe appetite meanes whereof come oftentymes theyr bane yee ſhall knowe diſeaſe yee giue hawke great gorge ſpecially ouer night next morning ſhe haue lyſt hir breakefaſt becommeth colde ſo falleth great diſeaſe mallopin booke prince giueth medicine yee perceyue hir ſo morfounded haue loſt hir appetite giue hir meate day ſet water hir let hir bowze bathe hir pleaſure ſhee hath bathed weathered agayne throwe hir liue pigeon let hir kill take much bloud ſhee lyſteth let hir eate paſt one legges tyme afterwarde ſet hir downe ſome high thing water hir beware giuing hir great gorge foure fiue dayes togyther giue hir fiue ſixe cloues mace lapped vp hennes ſkinne recouer hir diſeaſe called priuie hidden euill hawke vvhich vve haue ſpeciall terme sometymes hawkes periſhe want knowledge ſome ſecrete diſeaſe happeneth therefore tell ſhall know hawke hath diſeaſe alwayes greedie feede inſomuch ye haue giuen hir great gorge morning ſhee haue indewed hande ye giue hir another noone ſhee put ouer yee giue hir thirde night ſhee diſpatch quickly alſo ſhee feedeth greedie nippie ſhee diſeaſe commeth hawke verie poore lowe ſtate deſirous ſet hir vp quickly thinking bring hir good plight great gorge feed hir pigeon fleſhe ſhe cannot indew reaſon hir pouertie weakneſſe want heate liuer heate whereof cauſe kindly digeſtiō indewing alſo may know diſeaſe hir often muting wateriſh thin beſides ſhe doth ſliſe thā ſhe wot reaſon ſpedy induing hir meat maiſter mallopin booke prince ſayeth remedie diſeaſe yee muſte ſtiepe ſheepes heart cutte ſmall peeces one night aſſes milke goates milke next day giue hawke quarter morning hir beaching much noone reſt night forcing hir receyue much milke ye continue fiue ſix dayes togither till yee ſee hir mute kindely feede hir reaſonably good meate ſtieped oyle ſweete almondes continuing three foure dayes ſpace twice day ye find hawke mend ſo increaſe hir meales little little till ſhee bee good plight ſhe alwayes continuing ſayde mylke ſome opinion milke good diſeaſes hawke maſter amé caſsian ſaith remedie diſeaſe yee muſt take tortoys land water hir lynes criance fiſt fiſt vp perch bate hir wing ye may well thinke ſhe hath diſeaſe reynes therefore maiſter caſsian willeth chop hare ſkinne haire verie ſmall fine peeces mingle cattes fleſhe feede hawke ſeuen eight dayes togither ſhee indew ſhee ſhall recouer hir diſeaſe havvkes haue ague feuer knowe whither hawke haue ague marke whether hir feete bee ſwollen woont bee bee hath ſhee ague remedie miſchiefe michelin ſayeth muſte mingle arſenicke capon greace togyther well ſprinckled vineger whereof muſt make little ball whiche muſte cauſe hawke take caſting hir vſe ſuch wiſe ſhe may three foure dayes wyth kynde fleſh ſo ſeaſoned cure hir teynte hawkes feather hovve many kindes hitherto ye haue read inwarde diſeaſes hawkes nowe tell outwarde accidentes firſt ſpeake teynte whiche frenche falconer call taigne italian zignuole tarmae whereof three ſortes firſt theyr principalles long feather beginne droppe meanes whereof many hawkes marred caſt awaye without knowledge howe helpe maiſter amé caſsian ſayeth commeth ſometymes lyuer exceſſiue heate bodye meanes whereof ſmall pymples ryſe vppon theyr wing traynes whiche afterwarde cauſe theyr feather droppe gone hole ſtoode doe cloze agayne wherethrough hawke doeth periſhe ſhee bee remedyed diſeaſe contagious one take therefore yee muſte let hawke affected ſtande neare hawke ſounde neyther muſt touche feede ſounde hawke gloue whereon ſicke hawke hath beende fedde yee ſhall knowe ſhee hath diſeaſe hir often picking hir beake vppon hir principall feather hir wing trayne theyr dropping awaye therefore caſt hawke let hir bee well peruſed yee ſhall fynde ſayde diſeaſe remedie whereof maiſter martin maiſter caſsian ſay muſt caſt hawke haue ſound ſmall pimple whence feather dropt firſt muſte get little ſticke firre doe falleth ſometimes hawke cannot well indew put ouer hir meate ſhe ſhould doe onely bycauſe ſhe foule within hath taken ſome ſurfeyt elſe ſhe low poore hir keeper deſirous ſet hir vp againe haſhly gaue hir great gorge ſhe reaſon hir weakneſſe able put ouer indewe wherethrough ſhee ſurfetted forwent hir appetite feeding altogither remedie hereof mallopin ſayeth ye muſt feede hir light meates ſurfeyted wanteth naturall heate take verie pure white wine ſteepe hir meate luke warme giuing hir little little oft tymes day alwayes chaunging hir meate ſee light digeſtion doe thus hir till ſhe better tune againe giuing hir fiue ſixe cloues mace euening wrapped little cotton ſome ſuch like deuice warme hir head hir partes verie well let cotton bee dipped odoriferous olde wine hawke neither greedily vpon reaſon ſhe kept ouereager ſharp ſhe neither get vp downe thervpon falleth danger death wherfore men ought vſe diſcretion feeding hawkes ouergorge maſter caſsian ſayeth remedie thereof ye muſt ſet cleane water veſſell hawke let hir bowze thereof hir pleaſure ſhe liſt take quantitie beane porke fatteſt two part leſſe powder pepper little ſalte brayed verie ſmall ye haue mingled togither hir caſt hir gorge rub roofe hir mouth litle vineger pepper ſhe caſt ye liſt ye may alſo conuey two three droppes ſame hir naris make hir caſt hir gorge hande ye ſee vineger pepper vexe diſtemper hir meate falleth caſting ſoone ſhee hath receyued commeth feeding hir groſſe foule vnholeſome meate waſhed elſe ſhe foule panell ſo cannot indew reaſon great ſtore filth within hir therefore ye muſt againe nouriſhe well ye mind make hawke eager ſharpe ſet without bating hir ſelfe take hart liuer pye ye haue made powder make hawke eate ſette hir ſharpe eager theſe opinion frenche falconer consider vſe moſt probable election pleaſure hawke hath liſte flee become vnluſtie ſlouthfull nowe happeneth hawke hath lyſt flee eyther bicauſe ſhe euill keeping witte ſuche knowe howe gyue hir hir ryghtes bowzing bathing ſuche thing whereof ſometymes ſhee hath greate neede bycauſe hawke hyghe full greaſe wherethrough ſhee becommeth coye contrarywiſe bycauſe ſhee lowe poore elſe reaſon ſome miſhappe hawke ſicke diſeaſed ye may vſe remedy ſette downe heretofore according ſeuerall nature diſeaſes tyll hawke good plyght againe ſhe hawke hath broken hir wing ſome miſchaunce happeneth ſomewhile hawke breaketh hir wing miſchaunce bating againſt ground otherwiſe maſter mallopin ſayeth hawke hath hir wing broken manner yee muſte take sanguis draconis bole armoniacke gum arabicke white franckincenſe whiche called olibanum maſticke aloe cicotrine like quantitie reaſonable quantitie fine meale flower make powder ſayde thing tempering white egge make thereof playſter laye hurte yee haue firſte ſette
